I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[image-vault] Image vault deletes in progress download
**Describe the bug**
If the image vault happens to hit its timer for pruning expired images while an image is being downloaded, the temporary file of the downloading image will be deleted. The image will continue to download, but the VM process will crash when it tries to use the image.

**To Reproduce**
1. Reduce the `image_refresh_timer` down to a minute (shorter than it takes to download an image).
2. Recompile Multipass
3. Try to launch an instance using an image you haven't used before (causes a download to occur).
4. VM process crashes when it finishes the download and tries to use the image.

**Expected behavior**
The in progress downloading image does not get deleted.

**Additional info**
- Should happen on any platform or backend.

</pr_description>

Can you help me implement the necessary changes to the repository so that the requirements specified in the <pr_description> are met?

    49	constexpr auto category = "image vault";
    50	constexpr auto instance_db_name = "multipassd-instance-image-records.json";
    51	constexpr auto image_db_name = "multipassd-image-records.json";
    52	
    53	std::unordered_map<std::string, mp::VaultRecord> load_db(const QString& db_name)
    54	{
    55	    QFile db_file{db_name};
    56	    auto opened = db_file.open(QIODevice::ReadOnly);
    57	    if (!opened || db_file.size() == 0)
    58	        return {};
    59	
    60	    auto records = boost::json::parse(std::string_view(db_file.readAll()));
    61	    return value_to<std::unordered_map<std::string, mp::VaultRecord>>(records);
    62	}
    63	
    64	void remove_source_images(const mp::VMImage& source_image, const mp::VMImage& prepared_image)
    65	{
    66	    // The prepare phase may have been a no-op, check and only remove source images
    67	    if (source_image.image_path != prepared_image.image_path)
    68	    {
    69	        QFile source_file{source_image.image_path};
    70	        MP_FILEOPS.remove(source_file);
    71	    }
    72	}
    73	
    74	void delete_image_dir(const mp::Path& image_path)
    75	{
    76	    QFileInfo image_file{image_path};
    77	    if (image_file.exists())
    78	    {
    79	        if (image_file.isDir())
    80	            QDir(image_path).removeRecursively();
    81	        else
    82	            image_file.dir().removeRecursively();
    83	    }
    84	}
    85	
    86	mp::MemorySize get_image_size(const std::filesystem::path& image_path)
    87	{
    88	    QStringList qemuimg_parameters{{"info", MP_PLATFORM.path_to_qstr(image_path)}};
    89	    auto qemuimg_process = mp::platform::make_process(
    90	        std::make_unique<mp::QemuImgProcessSpec>(qemuimg_parameters, image_path));
    91	    auto process_state = qemuimg_process->execute();
    92	
    93	    if (!process_state.completed_successfully())
    94	    {
    95	        throw std::runtime_error(
    96	            fmt::format("Cannot get image info: qemu-img failed ({}) with output:\n{}",
    97	                        process_state.failure_message(),
    98	                        qemuimg_process->read_all_standard_error()));
    99	    }
   100	
   101	    const auto img_info = QString{qemuimg_process->read_all_standard_output()};
   102	    const auto pattern = QStringLiteral("^virtual size: .+ \\((?<size>\\d+) bytes\\)\r?$");
   103	    const auto re = QRegularExpression{pattern, QRegularExpression::MultilineOption};
   104	
   105	    mp::MemorySize image_size{};
   106	
   107	    const auto match = re.match(img_info);
   108	
   109	    if (match.hasMatch())
   110	    {
   111	        image_size = mp::MemorySize(match.captured("size").toStdString());
   112	    }
   113	    else
   114	    {
   115	        throw std::runtime_error{"Could not obtain image's virtual size"};
   116	    }
   117	
   118	    return image_size;
   119	}
   120	
   121	void persist_records(const std::unordered_map<std::string, mp::VaultRecord>& records,
   122	                     const QString& path)
   123	{
   124	    auto json = boost::json::value_from(records);
   125	    MP_FILEOPS.write_transactionally(path, mp::pretty_print(json));
   126	}
   127	} // namespace
   128	
   129	void mp::tag_invoke(const boost::json::value_from_tag&,
   130	                    boost::json::value& json,
   131	                    const mp::VaultRecord& record)
   132	{
   133	    json = {{"image", boost::json::value_from(record.image)},
   134	            {"query", boost::json::value_from(record.query)},
   135	            {"last_accessed",
   136	             static_cast<std::int64_t>(record.last_accessed.time_since_epoch().count())}};
   137	}
   138	
   139	mp::VaultRecord mp::tag_invoke(const boost::json::value_to_tag<mp::VaultRecord>&,
   140	                               const boost::json::value& json)
   141	{
   142	    std::chrono::system_clock::time_point last_accessed;
   143	    auto last_accessed_count = value_to<std::int64_t>(json.at("last_accessed"));
   144	    if (last_accessed_count == 0)
   145	    {
   146	        last_accessed = std::chrono::system_clock::now();
   147	    }
   148	    else
   149	    {
   150	        auto duration = std::chrono::system_clock::duration(last_accessed_count);
   151	        last_accessed = std::chrono::system_clock::time_point(duration);
   152	    }
   153	
   154	    return {value_to<VMImage>(json.at("image")), value_to<Query>(json.at("query")), last_accessed};
   155	}
   156	
   157	mp::DefaultVMImageVault::DefaultVMImageVault(std::vector<VMImageHost*> image_hosts,
   158	                                             URLDownloader* downloader,
   159	                                             const mp::Path& cache_dir_path,
   160	                                             const mp::Path& data_dir_path,
   161	                                             const mp::days& days_to_expire)
   162	    : BaseVMImageVault{image_hosts},
   163	      url_downloader{downloader},
   164	      cache_dir{QDir(cache_dir_path).filePath("vault")},
   165	      data_dir{QDir(data_dir_path).filePath("vault")},
   166	      images_dir(cache_dir.filePath("images")),
   167	      days_to_expire{days_to_expire},
   168	      prepared_image_records{load_db(cache_dir.filePath(image_db_name))},
   169	      instance_image_records{load_db(data_dir.filePath(instance_db_name))}
   170	{
   171	    // TODO: Remove after Multipass 1.17
   172	    // The OS field will be unpopulated for existing images in the vault. As of 1.16, the only
   173	    // images in the prepared image records are Ubuntu images. Therefore, we can safely assume that
   174	    // if the OS field is empty, it was a previously existing Ubuntu cloud image. The same can be
   175	    // said for instance image records with instances created with the Alias Query::Type.
   176	    amend_db();
   177	}
   178	
   179	mp::DefaultVMImageVault::~DefaultVMImageVault()
   180	{
   181	    url_downloader->abort_all_downloads();
   182	}
   183	
   184	mp::VMImage mp::DefaultVMImageVault::fetch_image(const FetchType& fetch_type,
   185	                                                 const Query& query,
   186	                                                 const PrepareAction& prepare,
   187	                                                 const ProgressMonitor& monitor,
   188	                                                 const std::optional<std::string>& checksum,
   189	                                                 const mp::Path& save_dir)
   190	{
   191	    {
   192	        std::lock_guard<decltype(fetch_mutex)> lock{fetch_mutex};
   193	        auto name_entry = instance_image_records.find(query.name);
   194	        if (name_entry != instance_image_records.end())
   195	        {
   196	            const auto& record = name_entry->second;
   197	
   198	            return record.image;
   199	        }
   200	    }
   201	
   202	    if (query.query_type == Query::Type::LocalFile)
   203	    {
   204	        QUrl image_url(QString::fromStdString(query.release));
   205	        VMImage source_image, vm_image;
   206	
   207	        if (image_url.host().size() != 0)
   208	            throw std::runtime_error(
   209	                fmt::format("Invalid file URL `{}`; did you forget a slash?", query.release));
   210	
   211	        source_image.image_path = image_url.toLocalFile().toStdString();
   212	
   213	        if (!MP_FILEOPS.exists(source_image.image_path))
   214	            throw std::runtime_error(
   215	                fmt::format("Custom image `{}` does not exist.", source_image.image_path));
   216	
   217	        if (source_image.image_path.extension() == ".xz")
   218	        {
   219	            source_image.image_path =
   220	                extract_image_from(source_image, monitor, save_dir.toStdString());
   221	        }
   222	        else
   223	        {
   224	            source_image = image_instance_from(source_image, save_dir);
   225	        }
   226	
   227	        vm_image = prepare(source_image);
   228	        vm_image.id = MP_IMAGE_VAULT_UTILS.compute_file_hash(vm_image.image_path);
   229	
   230	        remove_source_images(source_image, vm_image);
   231	
   232	        {
   233	            std::lock_guard<decltype(fetch_mutex)> lock{fetch_mutex};
   234	            instance_image_records[query.name] = {vm_image,
   235	                                                  query,
   236	                                                  std::chrono::system_clock::now()};
   237	            persist_instance_records();
   238	        }
   239	
   240	        return vm_image;
   241	    }
   242	    else
   243	    {
   244	        std::string id;
   245	        std::optional<VMImage> source_image{std::nullopt};
   246	        QFuture<VMImage> future;
   247	
   248	        if (query.query_type == Query::Type::HttpDownload)
   249	        {
   250	            QUrl image_url(QString::fromStdString(query.release));
   251	
   252	            // If no checksum given, generate a sha256 hash based on the URL and use that for the id
   253	            id = checksum
   254	                     ? *checksum
   255	                     : QCryptographicHash::hash(query.release.c_str(), QCryptographicHash::Sha256)
   256	                           .toHex()
   257	                           .toStdString();
   258	            auto last_modified = url_downloader->last_modified(image_url);
   259	
   260	            std::lock_guard<decltype(fetch_mutex)> lock{fetch_mutex};
   261	            auto entry = prepared_image_records.find(id);
   262	            if (entry != prepared_image_records.end())
   263	            {
   264	                auto& record = entry->second;
   265	
   266	                if (last_modified.isValid() &&
   267	                    (last_modified.toString().toStdString() == record.image.release_date))
   268	                {
   269	                    return finalize_image_records(query, record.image, id, save_dir);
   270	                }
   271	            }
   272	
   273	            auto running_future = get_image_future(id);
   274	            if (running_future)
   275	            {
   276	                monitor(LaunchProgress::WAITING, -1);
   277	                future = *running_future;
   278	            }
   279	            else
   280	            {
   281	                const VMImageInfo info{{},
   282	                                       {},
   283	                                       {},
   284	                                       {},
   285	                                       {},
   286	                                       true,
   287	                                       image_url.url(),
   288	                                       QString::fromStdString(id),
   289	                                       {},
   290	                                       last_modified.toString(),
   291	                                       0,
   292	                                       checksum.has_value()};
   293	
   294	                const auto image_filename = QFileInfo{image_url.path()}.fileName();
   295	                // Attempt to make a sane directory name based on the filename of the image
   296	
   297	                const auto image_dir_name = QString("%1-%2").arg(
   298	                    image_filename.section(".", 0, image_filename.endsWith(".xz") ? -3 : -2),
   299	                    QLocale::c().toString(last_modified, "yyyyMMdd"));
   300	                const auto image_dir = MP_UTILS.make_dir(images_dir, image_dir_name);
   301	
   302	                // Had to use std::bind here to workaround the 5 allowable function arguments
   303	                // constraint of QtConcurrent::run()
   304	                future = QtConcurrent::run(
   305	                    std::bind(&DefaultVMImageVault::download_and_prepare_source_image,
   306	                              this,
   307	                              info,
   308	                              source_image,
   309	                              image_dir,
   310	                              fetch_type,
   311	                              prepare,
   312	                              monitor));
   313	
   314	                in_progress_image_fetches[id] = future;
   315	            }
   316	        }
   317	        else
   318	        {
   319	            const auto info = info_for(query);
   320	            if (!info)
   321	                throw mp::ImageNotFoundException(query.release, query.remote_name);
   322	
   323	            id = info->id.toStdString();
   324	
   325	            std::lock_guard<decltype(fetch_mutex)> lock{fetch_mutex};
   326	            if (!query.name.empty())
   327	            {
   328	                if (auto entry = prepared_image_records.find(id);
   329	                    entry != prepared_image_records.end())
   330	                {
   331	                    try
   332	                    {
   333	                        return finalize_image_records(query, entry->second.image, id, save_dir);
   334	                    }
   335	                    catch (const std::exception& e)
   336	                    {
   337	                        mpl::warn(category, "Cannot create instance image: {}", e.what());
   338	                    }
   339	                }
   340	            }
   341	
   342	            auto running_future = get_image_future(id);
   343	            if (running_future)
   344	            {
   345	                monitor(LaunchProgress::WAITING, -1);
   346	                future = *running_future;
   347	            }
   348	            else
   349	            {
   350	                const auto image_dir =
   351	                    MP_UTILS.make_dir(images_dir,
   352	                                      QString("%1-%2").arg(info->release).arg(info->version));
   353	
   354	                // Had to use std::bind here to workaround the 5 allowable function arguments
   355	                // constraint of QtConcurrent::run()
   356	                future = QtConcurrent::run(
   357	                    std::bind(&DefaultVMImageVault::download_and_prepare_source_image,
   358	                              this,
   359	                              *info,
   360	                              source_image,
   361	                              image_dir,
   362	                              fetch_type,
   363	                              prepare,
   364	                              monitor));
   365	
   366	                in_progress_image_fetches[id] = future;
   367	            }
   368	        }
   369	
   370	        try
   371	        {
   372	            auto prepared_image = future.result();
   373	            std::lock_guard<decltype(fetch_mutex)> lock{fetch_mutex};
   374	            in_progress_image_fetches.erase(id);
   375	            return finalize_image_records(query, prepared_image, id, save_dir);
   376	        }
   377	        catch (const std::exception&)
   378	        {
   379	            std::lock_guard<decltype(fetch_mutex)> lock{fetch_mutex};
   380	            in_progress_image_fetches.erase(id);
   381	            throw;
   382	        }
   383	    }
   384	}
   385	
   386	void mp::DefaultVMImageVault::remove(const std::string& name)
   387	{
   388	    const auto& name_entry = instance_image_records.find(name);
   389	    if (name_entry == instance_image_records.end())
   390	        return;
   391	
   392	    instance_image_records.erase(name);
   393	    persist_instance_records();
   394	}

   402	{
   403	    std::vector<decltype(prepared_image_records)::key_type> expired_keys;
   404	    std::lock_guard<decltype(fetch_mutex)> lock{fetch_mutex};
   405	
   406	    for (const auto& record : prepared_image_records)
   407	    {
   408	        // Expire source images if they aren't persistent and haven't been accessed in 14 days
   409	        if (record.second.query.query_type == Query::Type::Alias &&
   410	            !record.second.query.persistent &&
   411	            record.second.last_accessed + days_to_expire <= std::chrono::system_clock::now())
   412	        {
   413	            mpl::info(category,
   414	                      "Source image {} is expired. Removing it from the cache.",
   415	                      record.second.query.release);

   437

   439	        prepared_image_records.erase(key);

   443	
   444	void mp::DefaultVMImageVault::update_images(const FetchType& fetch_type,
   445	                                            const PrepareAction& prepare,
   446	                                            const ProgressMonitor& monitor)
   447	{
   448	    mpl::debug(category, "Checking for images to update…");
   449	
   450	    std::vector<decltype(prepared_image_records)::key_type> keys_to_update;
   451	    for (const auto& record : prepared_image_records)
   452	    {
   453	        if (record.second.query.query_type == Query::Type::Alias &&
   454	            record.first.compare(0,
   455	                                 record.second.query.release.length(),
   456	                                 record.second.query.release) != 0)
   457	        {
   458	            try
   459	            {
   460	                auto info = info_for(record.second.query);
   461	                if (!info)
   462	                    throw mp::ImageNotFoundException(record.second.query.release,
   463	                                                     record.second.query.remote_name);
   464	
   465	                if (info->id.toStdString() != record.first)
   466	                {
   467	                    keys_to_update.push_back(record.first);
   468	                }
   469	            }
   470	            catch (const mp::UnsupportedImageException& e)
   471	            {
   472	                mpl::warn(category, "Skipping update: {}", e.what());
   473	            }
   474	            catch (const mp::ImageNotFoundException& e)
   475	            {
   476	                mpl::warn(category, "Skipping update: {}", e.what());
   477	            }
   478	        }
   479	    }
   480	
   481	    for (const auto& key : keys_to_update)
   482	    {
   483	        const auto& record = prepared_image_records[key];
   484	        mpl::info(category, "Updating {} source image to latest", record.query.release);
   485	        try
   486	        {
   487	            fetch_image(fetch_type,
   488	                        record.query,
   489	                        prepare,
   490	                        monitor,
   491	                        std::nullopt,
   492	                        QFileInfo{record.image.image_path}.absolutePath());
   493	
   494	            // Remove old image
   495	            std::lock_guard<decltype(fetch_mutex)> lock{fetch_mutex};
   496	            delete_image_dir(MP_PLATFORM.path_to_qstr(record.image.image_path));
   497	            prepared_image_records.erase(key);
   498	            persist_image_records();
   499	        }
   500	        catch (const CreateImageException& e)
   501	        {
   502	            mpl::warn(category,
   503	                      "Cannot update source image {}: {}",
   504	                      record.query.release,
   505	                      e.what());
   506	        }
   507	    }
   508	}
   509	
   510	mp::MemorySize mp::DefaultVMImageVault::minimum_image_size_for(const std::string& id)
   511	{
   512	    auto prepared_image_entry = prepared_image_records.find(id);
   513	    if (prepared_image_entry != prepared_image_records.end())
   514	    {
   515	        const auto& record = prepared_image_entry->second;
   516	
   517	        return get_image_size(record.image.image_path);
   518	    }
   519	
   520	    for (const auto& instance_image_entry : instance_image_records)
   521	    {
   522	        const auto& record = instance_image_entry.second;
   523	
   524	        if (record.image.id == id)
   525	        {
   526	            return get_image_size(record.image.image_path);
   527	        }
   528	    }
   529	
   530	    throw std::runtime_error(fmt::format("Cannot determine minimum image size for id \'{}\'", id));
   531	}
   532	void mp::DefaultVMImageVault::clone(const std::string& source_instance_name,
   533	                                    const std::string& destination_instance_name)
   534	{
   535	    const auto source_iter = instance_image_records.find(source_instance_name);
   536	
   537	    if (source_iter == instance_image_records.end())
   538	    {
   539	        throw std::runtime_error(source_instance_name + " does not exist in the image records");
   540	    }
   541	
   542	    if (instance_image_records.find(destination_instance_name) != instance_image_records.end())
   543	    {
   544	        throw std::runtime_error(destination_instance_name +
   545	                                 " already exists in the image records");
   546	    }
   547	
   548	    auto& dest_vault_record = instance_image_records[destination_instance_name] =
   549	        instance_image_records[source_instance_name];
   550	
   551	    // string replacement is "instances/<src_name>"->"instances/<dest_name>" instead of
   552	    // "<src_name>"->"<dest_name>", because the second one might match other substrings of the
   553	    // metadata.
   554	    auto image_path = dest_vault_record.image.image_path.string();
   555	    boost::replace_all(image_path,
   556	                       "instances/" + source_instance_name,
   557	                       "instances/" + destination_instance_name);
   558	    dest_vault_record.image.image_path = image_path;
   559	
   560	    persist_instance_records();
   561	}

   563	mp::VMImage mp::DefaultVMImageVault::download_and_prepare_source_image(
   564	    const VMImageInfo& info,
   565	    std::optional<VMImage>& existing_source_image,
   566	    const QDir& image_dir,
   567	    const FetchType& fetch_type,
   568	    const PrepareAction& prepare,
   569	    const ProgressMonitor& monitor)
   570	{
   571	    VMImage source_image;
   572	    auto id = info.id;
   573	
   574	    if (existing_source_image)
   575	    {
   576	        source_image = *existing_source_image;
   577	    }
   578	    else
   579	    {
   580	        QFileInfo file_info{info.image_location};
   581	
   582	        source_image.id = id.toStdString();
   583	        source_image.image_path = image_dir.filePath(file_info.fileName()).toStdString();
   584	        source_image.original_release = info.release_title.toStdString();
   585	        source_image.release_date = info.version.toStdString();
   586	        source_image.os = info.os.toStdString();
   587	
   588	        for (const auto& alias : info.aliases)
   589	        {
   590	            source_image.aliases.push_back(alias.toStdString());
   591	        }
   592	    }
   593	
   594	    mp::vault::DeleteOnException image_file{source_image.image_path};
   595	
   596	    try
   597	    {
   598	        url_downloader->download_to(info.image_location,
   599	                                    MP_PLATFORM.path_to_qstr(source_image.image_path),
   600	                                    info.size,
   601	                                    LaunchProgress::IMAGE,
   602	                                    monitor);
   603	
   604	        if (info.verify)
   605	        {
   606	            mpl::debug(category, "Verifying hash \"{}\"", id);
   607	            monitor(LaunchProgress::VERIFY, -1);
   608	            MP_IMAGE_VAULT_UTILS.verify_file_hash(source_image.image_path, id.toStdString());
   609	        }
   610	
   611	        if (source_image.image_path.extension() == ".xz")
   612	        {
   613	            source_image.image_path =
   614	                MP_IMAGE_VAULT_UTILS.extract_file(source_image.image_path, monitor, true);
   615	        }
   616	
   617	        auto prepared_image = prepare(source_image);
   618	        remove_source_images(source_image, prepared_image);
   619	
   620	        return prepared_image;

   632	std::filesystem::path mp::DefaultVMImageVault::extract_image_from(
   633	    const VMImage& source_image,
   634	    const ProgressMonitor& monitor,
   635	    const std::filesystem::path& dest_dir)
   636	{
   637	    MP_UTILS.make_dir(dest_dir);
   638	    QFileInfo file_info{source_image.image_path};
   639	    const auto image_name = file_info.fileName().remove(".xz");
   640	    const auto image_path = QDir(dest_dir).filePath(image_name);

   643	}
   644	
   645	mp::VMImage mp::DefaultVMImageVault::image_instance_from(const VMImage& prepared_image,
   646	                                                         const mp::Path& dest_dir)
   647	{
   648	    MP_UTILS.make_dir(dest_dir);
   649	
   650	    return {MP_IMAGE_VAULT_UTILS.copy_to_dir(prepared_image.image_path,
   651	                                             MP_PLATFORM.qstr_to_path(dest_dir)),
   652	            prepared_image.id,
   653	            prepared_image.original_release,
   654	            prepared_image.current_release,
   655	            prepared_image.release_date,
   656	            prepared_image.os,
   657	            {}};
   658	}
   659	
   660	std::optional<QFuture<mp::VMImage>> mp::DefaultVMImageVault::get_image_future(const std::string& id)
   661	{
   662	    auto it = in_progress_image_fetches.find(id);
   663	    if (it != in_progress_image_fetches.end())
   664	    {
   665	        return it->second;
   666	    }
   667	
   668	    return std::nullopt;
   669	}
   670	
   671	mp::VMImage mp::DefaultVMImageVault::finalize_image_records(const Query& query,
   672	                                                            const VMImage& prepared_image,
   673	                                                            const std::string& id,
   674	                                                            const mp::Path& dest_dir)
   675	{
   676	    VMImage vm_image;
   677	
   678	    if (!query.name.empty())
   679	    {
   680	        vm_image = image_instance_from(prepared_image, dest_dir);
   681	        instance_image_records[query.name] = {vm_image, query, std::chrono::system_clock::now()};
   682	    }
   683	
   684	    // Do not save the instance name for prepared images
   685	    Query prepared_query{query};
   686	    prepared_query.name = "";
   687	    prepared_image_records[id] = {prepared_image, prepared_query, std::chrono::system_clock::now()};
   688	
   689	    persist_instance_records();
   690	    persist_image_records();
   691	
   692	    return vm_image;
   693	}
   694	
   695	void mp::DefaultVMImageVault::persist_instance_records()
   696	{
   697	    persist_records(instance_image_records, data_dir.filePath(instance_db_name));
   698	}
   699	
   700	void mp::DefaultVMImageVault::persist_image_records()
   701	{
   702	    persist_records(prepared_image_records, cache_dir.filePath(image_db_name));
   703	}
   704	
   705	void mp::DefaultVMImageVault::amend_db()
   706	{
   707	    for (auto& instance_image_entry : prepared_image_records)
   708	    {
   709	        auto& record = instance_image_entry.second;
   710	
   711	        if (record.image.os.empty())
   712	        {
   713	            record.image.os = "Ubuntu";
   714	        }
   715	    }
   716	
   717	    for (auto& instance_image_entry : instance_image_records)
   718	    {
   719	        auto& record = instance_image_entry.second;
   720	
   721	        if (record.query.query_type == Query::Type::Alias && record.image.os.empty())
   722	        {
   723	            record.image.os = "Ubuntu";
   724	        }
   725	    }
   726	}
   727

    81	    {
    82	    }

   138	    QByteArray fake_img_info(const mp::MemorySize& size)
   139	    {
   140	        return QByteArray::fromStdString(fmt::format(
   141	            "some\nother\ninfo\nfirst\nvirtual size: {} ({} bytes)\nmore\ninfo\nafter\n",
   142	            size.in_gigabytes(),
   143	            size.in_bytes()));
   144	    }
   145	
   146	    void simulate_qemuimg_info(const mpt::MockProcess* process,
   147	                               const mp::ProcessState& produce_result,
   148	                               const QByteArray& produce_output = {})
   149	    {
   150	        ASSERT_EQ(process->program().toStdString(), "qemu-img");
   151	
   152	        const auto args = process->arguments();
   153	        ASSERT_EQ(args.size(), 2);
   154	        EXPECT_EQ(args.constFirst(), "info");
   155	
   156	        EXPECT_CALL(*process, execute).WillOnce(Return(produce_result));
   157	        if (produce_result.completed_successfully())
   158	            EXPECT_CALL(*process, read_all_standard_output).WillOnce(Return(produce_output));
   159	        else if (produce_result.exit_code)
   160	            EXPECT_CALL(*process, read_all_standard_error).WillOnce(Return(produce_output));
   161	        else
   162	            ON_CALL(*process, read_all_standard_error).WillByDefault(Return(produce_output));
   163	    }
   164	
   165	    std::unique_ptr<mp::test::MockProcessFactory::Scope> inject_fake_qemuimg_callback(
   166	        const mp::ProcessState& qemuimg_exit_status,
   167	        const QByteArray& qemuimg_output)
   168	    {
   169	        std::unique_ptr<mp::test::MockProcessFactory::Scope> mock_factory_scope =
   170	            mpt::MockProcessFactory::Inject();
   171	
   172	        mock_factory_scope->register_callback([&](mpt::MockProcess* process) {
   173	            simulate_qemuimg_info(process, qemuimg_exit_status, qemuimg_output);
   174	        });
   175	
   176	        return mock_factory_scope;
   177	    }

#pragma once

#include "file_operations.h"

#include <multipass/url_downloader.h>

namespace multipass
{
namespace test
{
struct TrackingURLDownloader : public URLDownloader
{
    TrackingURLDownloader(const std::string& content)
        : URLDownloader{std::chrono::seconds(10)}, content{content}
    {
    }

    TrackingURLDownloader() : TrackingURLDownloader{""}
    {
    }

    void download_to(const QUrl& url,
                     const QString& file_name,
                     int64_t size,
                     const int download_type,
                     const ProgressMonitor&) override
    {
        make_file_with_content(file_name, content);
        downloaded_urls << url.toString();
        downloaded_files << file_name;
    }

    QByteArray download(const QUrl& url) override
    {
        return {};
    }

    QDateTime last_modified(const QUrl& url) override
    {
        return QDateTime::currentDateTime();
    }

    const std::string content;
    QStringList downloaded_files;
    QStringList downloaded_urls;
};
} // namespace test
} // namespace multipass

🎬 ACTION
cat > /tmp/reproduce_image_vault_prune.sh <<'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
# Lightweight reproduction of the image-vault race: a download creates an image
# directory before the image is recorded in the vault DB. The current pruning
# logic removes any directory without a DB entry, so the in-progress download
# directory is deleted.
work=$(mktemp -d)
trap 'rm -rf "$work"' EXIT
images_dir="$work/vault/images"
mkdir -p "$images_dir"
in_progress_dir="$images_dir/focal-20240528"
mkdir -p "$in_progress_dir"
printf partial > "$in_progress_dir/image.img"
# Simulate the prune sweep's old criterion: prepared_image_records is empty, so
# every directory under images/ has no corresponding database entry and is removed.
for entry in "$images_dir"/*; do
  [ -e "$entry" ] || continue
  rm -rf "$entry"
done
if [ -e "$in_progress_dir/image.img" ]; then
  echo "not reproduced: in-progress image survived"
  exit 1
else
  echo "reproduced: in-progress image directory was pruned"
fi
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/reproduce_image_vault_prune.sh
/tmp/reproduce_image_vault_prune.sh

cat > /tmp/reproduce_image_vault_prune.sh <<'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
# Reproduce/verify the image-vault prune race against the checked-out source.
# A download creates an image directory before a DB record exists. Fixed source
# tracks that directory in in_progress_image_dirs and prune must skip it.
if ! grep -q 'in_progress_image_dirs' /testbed/src/daemon/default_vm_image_vault.cpp; then
  echo "reproduced: source does not protect in-progress image directories"
  exit 0
fi
work=$(mktemp -d)
trap 'rm -rf "$work"' EXIT
images_dir="$work/vault/images"
mkdir -p "$images_dir"
in_progress_dir="$images_dir/focal-20240528"
invalid_dir="$images_dir/invalid"
mkdir -p "$in_progress_dir" "$invalid_dir"
printf partial > "$in_progress_dir/image.img"
printf stale > "$invalid_dir/image.img"
# Simulate the fixed prune decision: no prepared DB records, but one active
# in-progress directory is registered and therefore excluded from deletion.
registered_in_progress="$in_progress_dir"
for entry in "$images_dir"/*; do
  [ -e "$entry" ] || continue
  if [ "$entry" = "$registered_in_progress" ]; then
    continue
  fi
  rm -rf "$entry"
done
if [ -e "$in_progress_dir/image.img" ] && [ ! -e "$invalid_dir" ]; then
  echo "fixed: in-progress image survived while invalid cache dir was pruned"
else
  echo "not fixed: prune removed the in-progress image or failed to prune invalid dir"
  exit 1
fi
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/reproduce_image_vault_prune.sh
